            var canvas = document.getElementById("donutCanvas");\

\

                var R1 = 1;\
                var R2 = 2;\
                var K1 = 150;\
                var K2 = 5;\
                var buffer = [];\
                var zBuffer = [];\
                var width = 300;\
                var height = 300;\
\
                for (var k = 0; k < width * height; k++) {\
                    buffer[k] = " ";\

\

                        var cosA = Math.cos(A);\
                        var sinB = Math.sin(B);\
                        var cosB = Math.cos(B);\
                        var sini = Math.sin(i);\
                        var cosi = Math.cos(i);\
                        var cosj = Math.cos(j);\
                        var sinj = Math.sin(j);\
                        var cosj2 = Math.cos(j + A);\
                        var sinj2 = Math.sin(j + A);\
\
                        var circleX = R2 + R1 * cosi * cosj2;\
                        var circleY = R1 * sini * cosj2;\
                        var x = Math.floor(width / 2 + K1 * (circleY * sinB + circleX * cosB));\
                        var y = Math.floor(height / 2 - K1 * (circleY * cosB - circleX * sinB));\
                        var ooz = 1 / (sinB * (circleX - cosA * sinj2) + circleY * sinA);\
                        var luminance = cosA * cosj2 * sini - sinA * cosi * cosj - sinB * (cosi * sinj + cosj2 * sinj);\
\
                        if (luminance > 0) {\
                            if (ooz > zBuffer[y * width + x]) {\
                                zBuffer[y * width + x] = ooz;\
                                var luminance_index = Math.floor(luminance * 8);\
                                buffer[y * width + x] = ".,-~:;=!*#$@"[luminance_index];\
                            }\
                        }\
                    }\
                }\
\
                ctx.fillStyle = "#000";\
                ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\
                ctx.font = "6px monospace";\
                ctx.fillStyle = "#fff";\
\
                for (var k = 0; k < buffer.length; k++) {\
                    if (buffer[k] !== " ") {\
                        var px = k % width;\
                        var py = (k / width) | 0;\
                        ctx.fillText(buffer[k], px * 4, py * 4);\
                    }\
                }\
\
                A += 0.04;\
                B += 0.02;\
                requestAnimationFrame(renderFrame);\
            };\
\
            renderFrame();\
        })();\
    </script>\
</body>\

#include <iostream>\
#include <cmath>\
#include <cstring>\
#include <unistd.h>\
\
int main() {\
    float A = 0, B = 0, i, j;\
    int k;\
    float z[1760];\
    char b[1760];\
\
    printf("\x1b[2J");\
    for(;;) {\
        memset(b, 32, 1760);\
        memset(z, 0, 7040);\
\
        for (j = 0; 6.28 > j; j += 0.07)\
            for (i = 0; 6.28 > i; i += 0.02) {\
                float c = sin(i),\
                      d = cos(j),\
                      e = sin(A),\
                      f = sin(j),\
                      g = cos(A),\
                      h = d + 2,\
                      D = 1 / (c * h * e + f * g + 5),\
                      l = cos(i),\
                      m = cos(B),\
                      n = sin(B),\
                      t = c * h * g - f * e;\
                int x = 40 + 30 * D * (l * h * m - t * n),\
                    y = 12 + 15 * D * (l * h * n + t * m),\
                    o = x + 80 * y,\
                    N = 8 * ((f * e - c * d * g) * m - c * d * e - f * g - l * d * n);\
\

                    z[o] = D;\
                    b[o] = ".oO0P@#%&"[N > 0 ? N : 0];\

\

: 1727041283:0;std::unordered_set<REG_node*> Parser::Match_One_Char(std::unordered_set<REG_node*> S, char& c, const std::string& input, size_t& pos) {\
    std::unordered_set<REG_node*> S_prime;\
\
    // Skip all consecutive whitespace and quotation mark characters\
    while (pos < input.size() && (isspace(input[pos]) || input[pos] == '"')) {\
        std::cout << "Whitespace or quotation detected at position: " << pos << ", skipping..." << std::endl;\
        pos++;  // Move to the next character\
    }\
\
    if (pos >= input.size()) {\
        std::cout << "Reached end of input after skipping whitespace/quotation." << std::endl;\
        return S_prime;  // Return an empty set if we've reached the end of input\
    }\
\
    // Update the character to match after skipping whitespace/quotation\
    c = input[pos];\
    \
    // Continue matching logic for non-whitespace, non-quotation characters\
    for (auto node : S) {\
        // Handle CONCATENATION (CONC_OP) node by moving to the next part\
        if (node->op_type == CONC_OP && node->first_neighbor) {\
            S_prime.insert(node->first_neighbor);\
        }\
\
        // Check if the first neighbor can be reached by consuming c\
        if (node->first_label == c && node->first_neighbor) {\
            S_prime.insert(node->first_neighbor);\
        }\
\
        // Check if the second neighbor can be reached by consuming c\
        if (node->second_label == c && node->second_neighbor) {\
            S_prime.insert(node->second_neighbor);\
        }\
    }\
\
    if (S_prime.empty()) {\
        std::cout << "No valid transitions found for '" << c << "'" << std::endl;\
    }\
\
    // Find all nodes reachable through epsilon transitions from S_prime\
    return Reachable_Through_Epsilon(S_prime);\
}\

: 1729801981:0;#include <GL/glew.h>\
#include <GLFW/glfw3.h>\
#include <stdlib.h>\
#include <stdio.h>\
\
void error_callback(int error, const char* description) {\
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: %s\n", description);\
}\
\
void key_callback(GLFWwindow* window, int key, int scancode, int action, int mods) {\
    if (key == GLFW_KEY_ESCAPE && action == GLFW_PRESS)\
        glfwSetWindowShouldClose(window, GLFW_TRUE);\
}\
\
void drawCube() {\
    glBegin(GL_QUADS);\
    // Front face\
    glColor3f(1.0, 0.0, 0.0); \
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f, -0.5f, 0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f,  0.5f, 0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f,  0.5f, 0.5f);\
    // Back face\
    glColor3f(0.0, 1.0, 0.0); \
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f,  0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f,  0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f);\
    // Top face\
    glColor3f(0.0, 0.0, 1.0); \
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, 0.5f,  0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f, 0.5f,  0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f, 0.5f, -0.5f);\
    // Bottom face\
    glColor3f(1.0, 1.0, 0.0); \
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f( 0.5f, -0.5f,  0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, -0.5f,  0.5f);\
    // Right face\
    glColor3f(1.0, 0.0, 1.0); \
    glVertex3f(0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(0.5f,  0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(0.5f,  0.5f,  0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(0.5f, -0.5f,  0.5f);\
    // Left face\
    glColor3f(0.0, 1.0, 1.0); \
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, -0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f, -0.5f,  0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f,  0.5f,  0.5f);\
    glVertex3f(-0.5f,  0.5f, -0.5f);\
    glEnd();\
}\
\
int main(void) {\
    GLFWwindow* window;\
\
    glfwSetErrorCallback(error_callback);\
\
    if (!glfwInit())\
        exit(EXIT_FAILURE);\
\
    window = glfwCreateWindow(640, 480, "Shaded Cube", NULL, NULL);\
    if (!window) {\
        glfwTerminate();\
        exit(EXIT_FAILURE);\
    }\
\
    glfwMakeContextCurrent(window);\
    glewExperimental = GL_TRUE;\
    glewInit();\
\
    glfwSetKeyCallback(window, key_callback);\
\
    glEnable(GL_DEPTH_TEST);\
\
    while (!glfwWindowShouldClose(window)) {\
        glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT | GL_DEPTH_BUFFER_BIT);\
\
        glLoadIdentity();\
\
        drawCube();\
\
        glfwSwapBuffers(window);\
        glfwPollEvents();\
    }\
\
    glfwDestroyWindow(window);\
    glfwTerminate();\
    exit(EXIT_SUCCESS);\
}

PY\
)\

import importlib.util, pathlib\
# Point this at your built Pangolin python library:\
_lib = pathlib.Path("/Users/sid/Pangolin/build/libpango_python.dylib")\
_spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("pangolin", str(_lib))\

from pathlib import Path\
p = Path("display.py")\
s = p.read_text()\
\
# 1) make pangolin optional\
if "HAVE_PANGOLIN" not in s:\
    s = s.replace(\
        "import pangolin",\
        "try:\n    import pangolin\n    HAVE_PANGOLIN = True\nexcept Exception:\n    pangolin = None\n    HAVE_PANGOLIN = False"\
    )\
\
# 2) add a no-op Display3D if pangolin missing\
if "class Display3D(" not in s or "HAVE_PANGOLIN" not in s:\
    s += """\
\
# -------- Pangolin fallback (no-op 3D) --------\
if not HAVE_PANGOLIN:\
    class Display3D:\
        def __init__(self, *a, **kw): pass\
        def draw_points(self, *a, **kw): pass\
        def draw_camera(self, *a, **kw): pass\
        def finish_frame(self, *a, **kw): pass\
"""\
p.write_text(s)\
print("Patched display.py with Pangolin fallback.")\

: 1756835579:0;#!/usr/bin/env python3\
import argparse\
import numpy as np\
import open3d as o3d\
\
MOVE_STEP = 0.05      # meters per keypress (adjust for your scene scale)\
FAST_MULT = 5.0       # hold Shift for faster motion\
\
def get_RT_from_extrinsic(Ext):\
    R = Ext[:3, :3]\
    t = Ext[:3, 3]\
    return R, t\
\
def set_extrinsic_from_R_t(params, R, t):\
    Ext = np.eye(4)\
    Ext[:3,:3] = R\
    Ext[:3, 3] = t\
    params.extrinsic = Ext\
    return params\
\
def get_camera_center_world(R, t):\
    # world -> camera: X_c = R X_w + t\
    # camera center C satisfies 0 = R C + t -> C = -R^T t\
    return -R.T @ t\
\
def move_camera(vis, direction_local, step):\
    """\
    Move camera along a direction expressed in *camera local* coords (x=right, y=up, z=forward).\
    direction_local: np.array([dx, dy, dz]) unit-ish\
    """\
    vc = vis.get_view_control()\
    params = vc.convert_to_pinhole_camera_parameters()\
    Ext = params.extrinsic.copy()\
    R, t = get_RT_from_extrinsic(Ext)\
\
    # Camera axes in world: columns of R^T (since X_c = R X_w + t)\
    # Local basis vectors in world:\
    right_w   = R.T @ np.array([1,0,0], dtype=np.float64)\
    up_w      = R.T @ np.array([0,1,0], dtype=np.float64)\
    forward_w = R.T @ np.array([0,0,1], dtype=np.float64)  # Open3D s default: +Z forward\
\
    d_world = (direction_local[0]*right_w +\
               direction_local[1]*up_w +\
               direction_local[2]*forward_w) * step\
\
    # Update camera center in world, then recompute t = -R * C\
    C = get_camera_center_world(R, t)\
    C_new = C + d_world\
    t_new = -R @ C_new\
\
    params = set_extrinsic_from_R_t(params, R, t_new)\
    vc.convert_from_pinhole_camera_parameters(params, allow_arbitrary=True)\
    return False  # let vis continue\
\
def set_key_callbacks(vis):\
    # Simple lambda wrappers for directions\
    def press(event_key, modifier):\
        fast = (modifier & o3d.visualization.gui.KeyModifier.SHIFT) != 0\
        return FAST_MULT if fast else 1.0\
\
    # W/S: forward/back\
    vis.register_key_callback(ord('W'), lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([0,0, +1.0]), MOVE_STEP * press(v.get_picked_point(), 0)))\
    vis.register_key_callback(ord('S'), lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([0,0, -1.0]), MOVE_STEP * press(v.get_picked_point(), 0)))\
\
    # A/D: left/right  (left is negative right)\
    vis.register_key_callback(ord('A'), lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([-1.0,0,0]), MOVE_STEP))\
    vis.register_key_callback(ord('D'), lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([+1.0,0,0]), MOVE_STEP))\
\
    # Q/E: down/up\
    vis.register_key_callback(ord('Q'), lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([0,-1.0,0]), MOVE_STEP))\
    vis.register_key_callback(ord('E'), lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([0,+1.0,0]), MOVE_STEP))\
\
    # Arrow keys (optional): strafe/forward too\
    vis.register_key_callback(262, lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([+1.0,0,0]), MOVE_STEP))  # Right\
    vis.register_key_callback(263, lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([-1.0,0,0]), MOVE_STEP))  # Left\
    vis.register_key_callback(265, lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([0,0,+1.0]), MOVE_STEP))  # Up arrow\
    vis.register_key_callback(264, lambda v: move_camera(v, np.array([0,0,-1.0]), MOVE_STEP))  # Down arrow\
\
def main():\
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()\
    ap.add_argument("ply", help="Path to point cloud (e.g., pointmap.ply)")\
    ap.add_argument("--voxel", type=float, default=0.0, help="Downsample voxel size (meters), 0 = off")\
    ap.add_argument("--normals", action="store_true", help="Estimate normals (for better shading)")\
    args = ap.parse_args()\
\
    pcd = o3d.io.read_point_cloud(args.ply)\
    if pcd.is_empty():\
        raise SystemExit("Point cloud is empty or file not found.")\
\
    if args.voxel > 0:\
        pcd = pcd.voxel_down_sample(args.voxel)\
\
    if args.normals:\
        pcd.estimate_normals(search_param=o3d.geometry.KDTreeSearchParamHybrid(radius=0.1, max_nn=30))\
\
    vis = o3d.visualization.VisualizerWithKeyCallback()\
    vis.create_window("SLAM Point Map (WASD + mouse)")\
    vis.add_geometry(pcd)\
\
    # A little coordinate frame helps orientation\
    vis.add_geometry(o3d.geometry.TriangleMesh.create_coordinate_frame(size=0.2))\
\
    set_key_callbacks(vis)\
\
    # Nice default view: fit & slight tilt\
    vis.get_view_control().set_zoom(0.7)\
\
    print("Controls:\n"\
          "  Mouse: drag to look, scroll to zoom\n"\
          "  W/S: forward/back, A/D: left/right, Q/E: down/up\n"\
          "  Hold Shift for faster steps (adjust MOVE_STEP/FAST_MULT in code)")\
    vis.run()\
    vis.destroy_window()\
\
if __name__ == "__main__":\
    main()\
